<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">冰凝</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font><font face="宋体">B+2000</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">动作：标准动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">能耗：</font><font face="宋体">3点意志力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">射程：以你为中心</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标：所有目标（不分敌我，不包括自己）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：底面直径</font><font face="宋体">6米，长度力量值*2米的圆柱形范围 </font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：立即</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：即使是最好的钢铁也会弯曲破碎，但是真男人的血肉是不屈的。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">对应龙语：</font><font face="宋体">Iiz（寒冰）Slen（血肉）Nus（雕塑）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你进行一次咆哮检定，造成检定成功数</font><font face="宋体">/点的可叠加的冻结点数，可以叠加。目标强韧豁免，但是每2点成功数只能豁免1点冻结点数。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">Iiz（寒冰）：学会龙语Iiz后，你使用本龙吼时可以获得增幅效果，你的胁迫技能等级每带来2点附加成功，则在施展本能力时，可以额外花费3点意志力，使目标的豁免检定再承受12DP减值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">Slen（血肉）：学会龙语Slen后，你的冰凝龙吼会对目标同时造成咆哮检定成功数/点寒冰严重伤害，该伤害以反射豁免，并承受对应减值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">Nus（雕塑）：学会龙语Nus后，若目标因承受冰凝龙吼的冻结点数而进入冰封状态，目标在该冰封状态下会陷入无助状态。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">=========================================================================================================== 
 </font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">龙魂觉醒</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font><font face="宋体">B+2000</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">动作：反射动作</font><font face="宋体">/迅捷动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">能耗：</font><font face="宋体">3点意志力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">射程：无</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标：自身</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：无</font> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：</font><font face="宋体">1分钟</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：你带上巨龙恐怖的外表，喷吐出炽热的气息，盔甲一般皮肤，发出愈发震耳欲聋的吼声。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">对应龙语：</font><font face="宋体">Mul（力量）Qua（铠甲）Diiv（龙）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你进行一次咆哮检定，并记录下成功数。在龙吼持续时间内，你获得本次咆哮检定成功数</font><font face="宋体">/点能量防御，当你进行近战攻击并且成功造成伤害时，你此次攻击会额外相当于你该次攻击造成伤害数的眩晕点数，无法叠加，目标强韧豁免，但是强韧豁免承受相当于你胁迫技能等级带来的附加成功数/点减值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">你在龙魂觉醒持续时间再度使用龙魂觉醒只会刷新龙魂觉醒的持续时间，并不会额外获得更多的成功数。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">Mul（力量）：学会龙语Mul后，龙魂觉醒期间，你的力量相关检定获得8DP能量加值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">Qua（铠甲）：学会龙语Qua后，龙魂觉醒期间，你免疫A级的接触攻击。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">Diiv（龙）：学会龙语Diiv后，龙魂觉醒期间，你的背后会出现远古龙裔的虚影，你获得8点全能量抗力。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">注意：</font><font face="宋体">“铠甲”和“龙”带来的效果全部基于本能力带来的能量防御，若该能量防御被破除，则龙语带来的对应效果也不再生效。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：无</font> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：</font><font face="宋体">“傲达威英！闻我吼声，赴我身旁。我在我需要之时召唤你。”</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">对应龙语：</font><font face="宋体">Od（霜雪）Ah（猎手）Viing（翅膀）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你可以以一个标准动作并消耗</font><font face="宋体">3点意志力召唤出霜翼猎手傲达威英来为你服务一段时间，你可以以一个反射动作或者迅捷动作遣散它——你必须妥善保护好它的生命，若其死亡，则你将永远失去本技能，除非重新购买。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">霜翼猎手傲达威英按照其先攻进行行动，被召唤出来的那一轮即可进行先攻检定并且按照先攻顺序进行行动，若其回合在当前回合之前，则其在你回合结束后可以立即行动一次，若本轮里你的回合也已经结束，则其在本轮所有单位均行动完毕后进行行动，并在下一轮按照先攻顺序进行正常行动。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">霜翼猎手傲达威英每轮同样具有自由动作、迅捷动作、移动动作和标准动作，轮到其行动时，你可以如同支配自己一般控制霜翼猎手傲达威英的行动。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">它具备如下属性：</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===================================================================</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt"><font face="宋体">生理系属性：力量</font><font face="宋体">12  敏捷6  耐力6</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">防御：天生防御</font><font face="宋体">9点，4点DR/神兵</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">天空之主：傲达威英获得等同其基础移动速度的飞行速度。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">巨龙吐息：以一个标准动作，傲达威英可以喷出自己的吐息，射程和范围为</font><font face="宋体">——以傲达威英的嘴巴为基底，直径6米，长度50米的圆柱形范围，造成19点火焰严重伤害，范围内所有目标以反射豁免。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">吐息结束后，傲达威英需要充能才可以再次吐息，回合开始时投掷</font><font face="宋体">1个1D10，若结果为8，9，10，则充能完成，可以立即进行吐息，战斗结束后，吐息充能自动完毕。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">霜翼猎手：在第一次召唤傲达威英时，你可以立即指定一项不超过</font><font face="宋体">B级别的龙吼（不得选取“巨龙呼唤”），傲达威英会立即获得它，一经选定不得更改（但是其不获得龙语效果）。注意，傲达威英施展的龙吼中的目标，若为“所有目标”，则也包括你在内。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">适当休息：傲达威英未被召唤时，视为处于长休息中，如常恢复其生命值。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">Od（霜雪）：学会龙语Od后，傲达威英的吐息造成的火焰伤害会无视目标的火焰能量抗力（全能量抗力如常生效）。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">Ah（猎手）：学会龙语Ah后，傲达威英的近战肉搏攻击获得4点附加成功。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">Viing（翅膀）：学会龙语Viing后，傲达威英的基础移动速度增加12米。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">=========================================================================================================== 
 </font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">延缓时间</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">价格：</font><font face="宋体">B+2000</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">动作：标准动作</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">能耗：</font><font face="宋体">3点意志力</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">射程：以你为中心</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">目标：所有目标（不分敌我，不包括自己）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">范围：半径力量值</font><font face="宋体">/米的球形范围</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">持续：</font><font face="宋体">2轮</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">描述：对时间吼叱，命令它遵从你的旨意，你周围的世界停止了。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">对应龙语：</font><font face="宋体">Tiid（时间）Klo（沙）Ul（永恒）</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">效果：你使范围内所有目标进行行动的动作需求上升</font><font face="宋体">1级（自由动作不受影响，反射动作/迅捷动作——移动动作；移动动作——标准动作；标准动作——整轮动作；整轮动作——全回合动作；全回合动作——无法执行）。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">这是一个</font><font face="宋体">B级别的时间效果，重复使用延缓时间龙吼并不会使受影响的目标的时间进一步延缓，只会刷新延缓时间龙吼的持续时间。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">这是一个不良状态。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">Tiid（时间）：学会龙语Tiid后，动作下降为自由动作开启。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">Klo（沙）： 
学会龙语Klo后，范围扩大至半径力量值*2米的球形范围。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 10.5pt; FONT-FAMILY: Calibri; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">Ul（永恒）：学会龙语Ul后，持续时间增加至5轮。</font></span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-pagination: widow-orphan"><span style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-font-kerning: 0.0000pt"><font face="宋体">===========================================================================================================
